### Post by SeijiSensei on 2016-02-27
The "Guest Additions" are now called the "Extension Pack," and yes, you need to install them to get a wider range of resolutions.

Click [here](http://download.virtualbox.org/virtualbox/5.0.14/Oracle_VM_VirtualBox_Extension_Pack-5.0.14-105127.vbox-extpack), and your browser should offer to install them using the VirtualBox Manager.  Then open the VM and choose Devices > Install Guest Additions CD.  You can then navigate to the ISO (usually under /media) then run VBoxLinuxAdditions.run.

In a Windows VM, you'll see the Extension Pack as a drive letter like D:\. 

Make sure your VM has an optical drive attached to one of the storage controllers, and that the drive is empty.  Use Settings in the VM Manager to check this.

### Post by MAFoElffen on 2016-02-29
For the extension pack, once you have the correct version downloaded (needs to be for the correct host OS, arch (32 or 64 bit) and for the matching version of VirtualBox), then if you go to the folder where it is located and double click on it... the file iis asociated to open with VirtualBox... and VirtualBox will install it as an extension of the main hypervisor (instead of just to a specific VM)...

You can also install it from a terminal using VBoxManage
```

sudo VBoxManage extpack install Oracle_VM_VirtualBox_Extension_Pack-4.3.12-93733.vbox-extpack

```

### Post by MAFoElffen on 2016-03-04
The extension pack gets installed to the host system/ the system running the hypervisor and hosting the guest VMs. The Guest Additions ISO [COLOR=#ff0000]"used to get"*[/COLOR] mounted in the Virtual CD drive of the VM.

[COLOR=#ff0000]***[/COLOR] But someone else tell me if I'm wrong (because I don't use VirtualBox every day anymore, so not as often as I used to)... Is the Guest Additions ISO's needed any longer? I thought they came out with the Extension Pack as a "Replacement For"... In Lieu of. Because I have fresh recent installs in VirtualBox, on both Linux and Windows hosts, both Linux and Windows guests... without the Guest Additions ISO. But I do have the Extension Pack installed on both Winodws and Linux Hosts... 

And the guests will install without the exetension pack's installed, just for additional porting (usb ports of host, extended video, share host folders) to the host.

---

### Post by kurt18947 on 2016-03-05
Here is something to check. With a guest O.S. running, click on 'file' on the virtualbox menu above the guest O.S. window, then 'preferences' -> 'display'.  Make sure that 'maximum guest screen size' is set properly. i have 'none' selected. Also on that menu 'machine' -> settings -> display I have video memory set as high as it will go and 3D acceleration selected.

---
